### [64] [SuCo: Sufficiency-guided Continuous Adaptive Reasoning](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17687v1)
*Jiahao Wang,Bingyu Liang,Chenhao Hu,Longhui Zhang,Xuebo Liu,Min zhang,Jing Li,Xuelong Li*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 充分性引导自适应推理框架，RL优化推理长度，可迁移至agent推理控制

TL;DR: 本文提出最小充分CoT（MSC）和两阶段训练框架SuCo，通过动态控制推理长度，在保持准确性的同时提高推理效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LRMs生成过长CoT导致计算浪费，现有方法缺乏何时推理足够的原理性准则。

Method: 定义MSC为最短充分CoT前缀，提出SuCo框架，包括MFT（使用自适应阈值构造MSC数据进行微调）和SAPO（通过强化学习优化推理长度，奖励充分性并惩罚过/欠思考）。

Result: 在数学、代码和科学基准上，SuCo同时提升了准确率和推理效率。

Conclusion: SuCo是一种有效的推理控制框架，能够实现准确性与效率的平衡。

中文摘要：尽管在复杂任务上表现卓越，大型推理模型（LRMs）常常生成过长的思维链（CoT），即使对于简单查询也会增加计算成本。现有的缓解这种低效率的工作通常依赖于离散的推理模式或固定的预算层级，缺乏何时推理足够的原理性标准。在这项工作中，我们引入了最小充分CoT（MSC），定义为CoT轨迹中最短的前缀，足以产生正确答案。我们实验证明，MSC不仅能减少推理标记，还能在不同难度级别上提高准确率。基于MSC，我们提出了充分性引导的连续自适应推理（SuCo），一个两阶段训练框架，用于沿着连续谱进行自主推理控制。在第一阶段，MSC对齐微调（MFT）使用问题自适应充分性阈值构建MSC数据，该阈值自然地随问题难度缩放，然后微调模型以内化简洁但充分的推理模式。在第二阶段，充分性感知策略优化（SAPO）通过强化学习进一步优化模型，具有动态复杂度跟踪和充分性感知奖励，惩罚过度思考和思考不足。在数学、代码和科学基准测试上的广泛实验表明，SuCo在准确性和推理效率上始终取得改进。

Original abstract: Despite remarkable performance on complex tasks, Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) often generate excessively long Chain-of-Thoughts (CoT), inflating computational costs even for simple queries. Existing efforts to mitigate this inefficiency typically rely on discrete reasoning modes or fixed budget tiers, lacking a principled criterion of when reasoning is sufficient. In this work, we introduce Minimal Sufficient CoT (MSC), defined as the shortest prefix of a CoT trajectory which is adequate for producing the correct answer. We empirically show that MSC not only reduces reasoning tokens, but also improves accuracy across difficulty levels. Building on MSC, we propose Sufficiency-guided Continuous Adaptive Reasoning (SuCo), a two-stage training framework for autonomous reasoning control along a continuous spectrum. In stage 1, MSC-Aligned Fine-Tuning (MFT) constructs MSC data using problem-adaptive sufficiency thresholds that naturally scale with question difficulty, then fine-tunes the model to internalize concise yet sufficient reasoning patterns. In stage 2, Sufficiency-Aware Policy Optimization (SAPO) further optimizes the model through reinforcement learning with dynamic complexity tracking and sufficiency-aware rewards that penalize both over- and under-thinking. Extensive experiments across mathematics, code, and science benchmarks show that SuCo consistently achieves improvements in both accuracy and reasoning efficiency.

</details>


### [65] [RubricsTree: Scalable and Evolving Open-Ended Evaluation of Personal Health Agents across Health Memory and Medical Skills](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18203v1)
*Weizhi Zhang,Zechen Li,Hamid Palangi,Ben Graef,A. Ali Heydari,Simon A. Lee,Salman Rahman,Ray Luo,Zeinab Esmaeilpour,Erik Schenck,Chloe Zhang,Yamin Li,Menglian Zhou,Philip S. Yu,Daniel McDuff,Lindsey Sunden,Mark Malhotra,Shwetak Patel,Ahmed A. Metwally*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: 健康agent评估框架，含层次化评注与自适应路由，可迁移至agent评测

TL;DR: RubricsTree是一个可扩展的评估框架，通过专家对齐的分层布尔评价标准和上下文自适应路由器，为个人健康AI提供可审计的评估，并在HealthBench上实现高达66%的相对性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决个人健康AI评估中医生注释成本高且不可扩展，以及LLM作为评判者主观、不一致、临床对齐不足的问题。

Method: 构建包含100多个原子布尔评价标准的专家对齐分层分类法，通过人机协同从4000个真实用户查询中演化；使用上下文感知自适应路由器激活相关加权子集，实现可扩展评估。

Result: 在专家对齐上显著超过强基线；可靠惩罚上下文退化响应；作为结构化指令、文本反馈或训练奖励时，在HealthBench上为Gemini、GPT和Qwen模型家族带来高达66%的相对性能提升。

Conclusion: RubricsTree为产品级个人健康AI提供了可扩展、可审计且可演化的评估基础设施，支持持续优化。

中文摘要：基于大语言模型的个人健康代理结合用户健康（传感器）指标，为缓解全球医疗资源获取不平等提供了有希望的途径。然而，大规模临床部署仍受限于一个开放式的评估瓶颈：医生注释可靠但成本高昂且不可扩展，而LLM作为评判者的评估虽可扩展但主观、不一致，有时甚至与临床对齐不佳。我们引入RubricsTree，一个可扩展的评估框架，包含由专家对齐的分层分类法，涵盖100多个原子的、临床可验证的布尔评价标准，这些标准通过迭代的人机协同协议，在一位经验丰富医生领导的专家小组指导下，从4000个真实用户查询中演化而来。一个上下文感知的自适应路由器仅激活每个查询相关的自动加权评价标准子集，从而提供可扩展评估所需的吞吐量，同时保持专家对齐的质量。通过系统性的元评估，我们证明RubricsTree（i）在具有挑战性的开放式查询上，其专家对齐程度显著超过一个强大规模评估基线；（ii）可靠地惩罚上下文退化的响应；（iii）当用作结构化指令、文本反馈或性能优化的训练奖励时，在HealthBench上为Gemini、GPT和Qwen模型家族带来高达约66%的相对提升。因此，RubricsTree提供了产品级个人健康AI持续优化所需的可扩展、可审计且不断演化的评估基础设施。

Original abstract: The LLM-empowered personal health agents with user health (sensor) metrics have offered a promising pathway to alleviate global disparities in healthcare access. However, large-scale clinical deployment remains constrained by an open-ended evaluation bottleneck: physician annotation is reliable but costly and unscalable, while LLM-as-a-judge evaluators are scalable but subjective, inconsistent, and sometimes clinically misaligned. We introduce RubricsTree, a scalable evaluation framework with an expert-aligned hierarchical taxonomy of over 100 atomic, clinically-verifiable Boolean rubrics, evolving from the insights of 4,000 real user queries through an iterative human-in-the-loop curation protocol with an expertise panel led by an experienced physician. A context-aware adaptive router activates only the relevant auto-weighted rubric subset per query, providing the throughput needed for scalable evaluation with expert-aligned quality. Through a systematic meta-evaluation, we show that RubricsTree (i) substantially exceeds a strong large-scale evaluation baseline in expert alignment on challenging open-ended queries; (ii) reliably penalizes contextually degraded responses; and (iii) when used as structured instructions, text feedback, or training rewards for performance optimization, yields up to ~66% relative gains on HealthBench for Gemini, GPT, and Qwen model families. RubricsTree thus provides a scalable, auditable, and evolving evaluation infrastructure required for the continuous optimization of product-level personal healthcare AI.

</details>


### [66] [ReproRepo: Scaling Reproducibility Audits with GitHub Repository Issues](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18237v1)
*Shanda Li,Qiuhong Anna Wei,Jingwu Tang,Valerie Chen,Nihar B Shah,Tim Dettmers,Yiming Yang,Ameet Talwalkar*

Main category: cs.CL

Selection reason: LLM agent代码审计框架，利用GitHub issues，直接相关coding agent

TL;DR: 提出了ReproRepo框架，利用GitHub issues自动评估LLM代理在论文再现性方面的能力。在1149篇论文上测试，最佳代理（Codex + GPT-5.5）能识别约90%论文的再现性问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有再现性评估基准依赖大量人工，难以扩展。需要自动化、可扩展的方法来评估LLM代理在现实再现性审计中的表现。

Method: 构建ReproRepo框架，收集人类在GitHub中提出的问题作为自然监督，实例化于1149篇机器学习论文，评估四种LLM代理配置（如Codex with GPT-5.5）识别再现性问题的能力。

Result: 最佳代理能识别约90%论文的至少一个语义相关人类报告障碍；代理在发现可见故障和识别正确语义区域方面有效，但精确定位能力不足。

Conclusion: ReproRepo是可扩展的再现性评估框架，可用于未来LLM代理在真实世界再现性审计的评估。

中文摘要：再现论文和发布代码的研究结果对于科学进步至关重要。现有工作引入了基准测试来评估LLM代理是否能够帮助再现性，但由于数据整理和评估需要大量人工努力，这些基准难以扩展。我们提出了ReproRepo，一个可扩展的再现性评估框架，利用人类提出的GitHub问题作为真实再现障碍的自然监督。我们在来自主要会议的1149篇近期机器学习论文上实例化ReproRepo，并评估了四种前沿模型-代理配置。我们的结果表明，即使不执行代码，LLM代理也能从论文-仓库对中识别出许多真实世界的再现性问题：我们研究中的最佳代理，即带有GPT-5.5的Codex，为约90%的研究论文找出了至少一个语义相关的人类报告障碍。进一步分析表明，代理在发现可见故障和识别正确语义区域方面特别有效，但在精确定位方面可能仍有不足。ReproRepo可以作为一个可重用的、可扩展的框架，用于未来对LLM代理在真实世界再现性审计中的评估。我们的代码已在https://github.com/LithiumDA/ReproRepo发布。

Original abstract: Reproducing research results from papers and released code is central to scientific progress. Existing works have introduced benchmarks to evaluate whether LLM agents can assist with reproducibility, but they are difficult to scale due to their reliance on substantial manual effort for data curation and evaluation. We introduce ReproRepo, a scalable framework for reproducibility evaluation that leverages human-raised GitHub issues as naturally occurring supervision on realistic reproduction blockers. We instantiate ReproRepo on 1,149 recent machine learning papers from major conferences and evaluate four frontier model-agent configurations. Our results show that LLM agents, even without executing code, can identify many real-world reproducibility problems from paper-repository pairs: the best agent in our study, namely Codex with GPT-5.5, surfaces at least one semantically related human-reported blocker for ~90% of papers in the study. Further analysis shows that agents are particularly effective for surfacing visible failures and identifying the right semantic region, but may still be insufficient in exact localization. ReproRepo can serve as a reusable, scalable framework for future evaluations of LLM agents on real-world reproducibility auditing. Our code is released at https://github.com/LithiumDA/ReproRepo.

</details>

# stat.OT [[Back]](#toc)

### [67] [A Variational Framework for LLM Generator-Regulator Games](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18424v1)
*Quanyan Zhu*

Main category: stat.OT

Selection reason: 提供生成器-调节器博弈理论框架，对agent安全与效用权衡有启发。

TL;DR: 提出了一个变分框架，将语言生成中的调控建模为生成器与判别器之间的博弈，从而在效用、熵和调控对齐之间取得平衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的语言生成调控方法缺乏统一的理论基础，亟需一个变分框架来形式化建模生成器与调控器之间的交互。

Method: 从自回归采样的诱导分布出发，将其与熵正则化吉布斯定律关联；将调控建模为最优判别器（其凸对偶值为f-散度），并通过鞍点问题表述生成器-调控器交互。

Result: 通过审查过滤和钓鱼防御两个案例研究，展示了框架如何评估效用、熵、散度、接收方分数和检测概率。

Conclusion: 该框架阐明了效用、熵、调控对齐与可检测性之间的权衡，为受调控语言生成提供了理论支持。

中文摘要：本文开发了一个用于受调控语言生成的变分框架。从自回归标记采样出发，我们推导出完整消息上的诱导分布，并将其与熵正则化的吉布斯定律联系起来。调控被建模为一个最优判别器，其凸对偶值为f-散度，而生成器-调控器交互被表述为一个鞍点问题。该框架适用于审核、审查、AI欺骗检测、合规审查、钓鱼防御和操纵控制，其中调控涉及可能消息的分布而非单个输出。均衡阐明了效用、熵、调控对齐和有限长度可检测性之间的权衡。两个有限词汇案例研究，审查过滤和钓鱼防御，说明了如何通过效用、熵、散度、接收方分数和检测概率来评估该理论。

Original abstract: This paper develops a variational framework for regulated language generation. Starting from autoregressive token sampling, we derive the induced distribution over complete messages and relate it to an entropy-regularized Gibbs law. Regulation is modeled as an optimal discriminator whose convex-dual value is an f-divergence, and the generator-regulator interaction is formulated as a saddle-point problem. The framework applies to moderation, censorship, AI deception detection, compliance auditing, phishing defense, and manipulation control, where regulation concerns a distribution over possible messages rather than a single output. The equilibrium clarifies the tradeoff among utility, entropy, regulatory alignment, and finite-length detectability. Two finite-vocabulary case studies, censorship filtering and phishing defense, illustrate how the theory can be evaluated through utility, entropy, divergence, receiver-side scores, and detection probability.

</details>

### [68] [When the Next Step Is Not One Step: Distribution-Aware Execution Modeling for Concurrent Go Programs](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17508v1)
*Kaviru Hapuarachchi*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 利用并发程序中的非确定性作为训练信号，通过多次运行聚合分布并微调模型，在预测Go程序下一步方面取得更好准确率和校准效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 并发程序因调度器非确定性导致预测困难，传统单标签训练效果不佳。

Method: 多次运行程序获得下一事件的经验分布，用KL散度微调7B模型匹配该分布。

Result: 在798个真实生产Go错误上，微调模型准确率36.2%，优于基线，且降低校准误差。

Conclusion: 分布训练有效且更可靠，同时发现goroutine泄漏形式特征。

中文摘要：训练模型预测并发程序中的下一步比看起来更难：同一个程序从同一个跟踪前缀开始两次运行可以产生不同的下一个事件，两者都有效，因为调度器是非确定性的。针对单个标签训练的模型是在学习猜测随机过程的一个结果。我们反过来利用非确定性作为训练信号。我们多次运行每个程序，将观察到的下一个事件聚合成经验分布，并使用KL散度目标微调一个7B模型以匹配该分布。在从真实生产Go错误（CockroachDB、Kubernetes、gRPC、etcd）中抽取的798个保留预测上，基于不到一千条轨迹的微调达到了36.2%的准确率，超过了零样本的Gemini 3.5 Flash（34.8%）和未微调的同一模型（28.6%）。分布训练在准确率上与交叉熵相匹配（35.8% vs. 36.2%），同时将期望校准误差从0.205降低到0.169。我们还为一种select阻塞的goroutine推导出一个正式的goroutine泄漏特征，其中P(GoUnblock)=0是由调度器语义保证的，而非学习得到的。我们发布了数据集、训练好的适配器和所有工具。

Original abstract: Training a model to predict the next step in a concurrent program is harder than it looks: two runs of the same program from the same trace prefix can produce different next events, both valid, because the scheduler is nondeterministic. A model trained against a single label is learning to guess one outcome of a random process. We turn this around and use the nondeterminism as a training signal. We run each program many times, aggregate the observed next events into an empirical distribution, and fine-tune a 7B model to match that distribution with a KL objective. On 798 held-out predictions drawn from real production Go bugs (CockroachDB, Kubernetes, gRPC, etcd), fine-tuning on fewer than a thousand traces reaches 36.2% accuracy, ahead of Gemini 3.5 Flash used zero-shot (34.8%) and the same model without fine-tuning (28.6%). Distribution training matches cross-entropy on accuracy (35.8% vs. 36.2%) while reducing Expected Calibration Error from 0.205 to 0.169. We also derive a formal goroutine-leak signature for a class of select-blocked goroutines where P(GoUnblock)=0 holds by scheduler semantics, not by learning. We release the dataset, trained adapters, and all tooling.

</details>


### [69] [Offline Preference-Based Trajectory Evaluation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17541v1)
*Fernando Diaz*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 提出基于偏好的轨迹评估方法，提升agent评测区分度，可迁移到代码agent评估。

TL;DR: 提出基于偏好的轨迹评估方法，减少平局、提升区分能力，揭示基准饱和可能源于评估度量选择。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统成功度量丢弃部分进展信息，导致大量平局和统计低效，难以区分系统性能。

Method: 通过时间进展和返回时间分布的时间偏好直接比较轨迹。

Result: 在多个基准上，成功度量有75%平局，轨迹偏好减少到35%，提升区分力、排名稳定性和数据效率。

Conclusion: 基准饱和不仅源于数据或难度，评估度量选择也是重要因素。

中文摘要：离线评估智能体系统通常将轨迹简化为最终成功，丢弃了部分进展的信息并导致广泛的平局，通过减少有效样本量和削弱区分系统的能力，造成了显著的统计低效。我们提出基于偏好的轨迹评估，通过时间上的进展和返回时间分布的时间偏好直接比较轨迹。我们发现，在多种智能体和交互基准测试中，标准的基于成功的度量在约75%的实例中产生平局比较，而轨迹感知偏好将平局减少到约35%，提高了区分能力、排名稳定性和数据效率。我们的结果表明，通常归因于数据收集不佳或问题难度的基准饱和，也可能由评估度量的选择来解释。

Original abstract: Offline evaluation of agentic systems often collapses trajectories to terminal success, discarding information about partial progress and inducing widespread ties, creating substantial statistical inefficiency by reducing effective sample size and weakening the ability to distinguish systems. We propose preference-based trajectory evaluation, which compares trajectories directly through temporal preferences over progress and time-to-return profiles. We find that, across diverse agentic and interactive benchmarks, standard success-based metrics produce tied comparisons on roughly 75% of instances, whereas trajectory-aware preferences reduce ties to roughly 35%, improving discriminative power, ranking stability, and data efficiency. Our results suggest that benchmark saturation, often attributed to poor data collection or problem difficulty, may also be explained by the choice of evaluation measure.

</details>


### [70] [ASTRA: A Scalable Next-Generation ATCO Training Simulator with Autonomous Simpilots](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18319v2)
*Ethan Chew,Enjia Wu,Iruss Eng,Ian Lim,Ranen Sim,Brandon Koh,Kaleb Nim,Caden Toh,Wei Dong Soin,Darius Koh,Galen Tay,Prannaya Gupta,Jonathan Koong,Yong Zhi Lim*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: ASTRA是一个端到端培训模拟器，通过微调ASR和本地自适应语音模型，显著降低新加坡口音航空语音的词错误率，并集成AI评估框架，提升培训效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有ATCO培训依赖人类培训师，且自动化系统对新加坡口音表现差，WER高达107.80%，需改进。

Method: 开发ASTRA系统，包含ASR转录、指令解释、语音生成流程，使用微调模型和本地自适应；并集成AI评估框架。

Result: ASR的WER降至23.45%，评估框架在准确性、简洁性、完整性上分别达到91.7%、88.2%、86.9%。

Conclusion: ASTRA实现可扩展标准化评估，减少教员工作量，优于现有方法。

中文摘要：空中交通管制员（ATCO）在确保空中交通安全、有序和高效运行方面至关重要，但培训能力受限于对专业人类培训师（称为simplot）的依赖，这些培训师必须在模拟空域中同时扮演飞行员和管制员的角色。现有的自动化解决方案依赖于以西方为中心的语音模型，这些模型在新加坡运营环境中表现不佳，现成的系统在新加坡口音的航空语音上显示出高达107.80%的词错误率（WER）。我们引入了ASTRA，一个端到端的培训模拟器，通过一个将ATCO语音转录、解释指令并使用本地自适应语音模型生成适当的飞行员和ATCO响应的流程，自动化了这些simplot角色。我们微调的自动语音识别（ASR）流程将WER降低到23.45%，在该领域显著优于现有方法。除了交通模拟，ASTRA还集成了一个AI辅助的性能评估框架，用于评估学员的无线电通信的准确性、简洁性和完整性，优化后分别达到91.7%、88.2%和86.9%的分数。该系统建立在DSPy和Unsloth等开源基础上，能够实现可扩展、标准化的ATCO评估，同时减少教员的工作量。

Original abstract: Air Traffic Control Operators (ATCOs) are vital in ensuring the safe, orderly, and efficient flow of air traffic, yet training capacity is constrained by reliance on specialized human trainers known as simpilots, who must role-play both pilots and ATCOs in a simulated airspace. Existing automated solutions rely on Western-centric speech models that perform poorly in Singaporean operational contexts, with off-the-shelf systems exhibiting Word Error Rates (WER) of up to 107.80% on Singaporean-accented aviation speech. We introduce ASTRA, an end-to-end training simulator that automates these simpilot roles through a pipeline that transcribes ATCO speech, interprets instructions, and generates appropriate pilot and ATCO responses using locally adapted voice models. Our fine-tuned Automatic Speech Recognition (ASR) pipeline reduces WER to 23.45%, substantially outperforming existing approaches in this domain. Beyond traffic simulation, ASTRA incorporates an AI-assisted performance evaluation framework that assesses trainee radiotelephony communications across accuracy, brevity, and completeness, achieving post-optimization scores of 91.7%, 88.2%, and 86.9%, respectively. Built on open-source foundations such as DSPy and Unsloth, this approach enables scalable, standardized ATCO assessment while reducing instructor workload.

### [71] [LoopCoder-v2: Only Loop Once for Efficient Test-Time Computation Scaling](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18023v1)
*Jian Yang,Shawn Guo,Wei Zhang,Tianyu Zheng,Yaxin Du,Haau-Sing Li,Jiajun Wu,Yue Song,Yan Xing,Qingsong Cai,Zelong Huang,Chuan Hao,Ran Tao,Xianglong Liu,Wayne Xin Zhao,Mingjie Tang,Weifeng Lv,Ming Zhou,Bryan Dai*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 循环Transformer代码生成agent，SWE-bench性能强，直接相关自动代码优化

TL;DR: 并行循环Transformer通过损失-收益权衡解释了为什么两循环最优，更多循环会导致性能下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究循环Transformer中循环次数的影响，特别是并行循环Transformer（PLT）中因跨循环位置偏移（CLP）带来的收益-成本权衡。

Method: 训练不同循环次数的LoopCoder-v2（7B PLT代码模型），从18T token从头训练，然后进行指令微调和评估。

Result: 两循环变体在代码生成、推理、智能体等任务上显著优于无循环基线（SWE-bench提升21.4点，Multi-SWE提升17点），但三循环及以上性能下降，呈现非单调性。

Conclusion: PLT的最优循环次数为2，受收益-成本权衡驱动：循环2提供主要优化，后续循环收益递减且CLP成本固定，导致饱和。

中文摘要：循环Transformer通过重复应用共享块来扩展潜在计算，但顺序循环会增加延迟和KV缓存内存（随循环次数增加）。并行循环Transformer（PLT）通过跨循环位置偏移（CLP）和共享KV门控滑动窗口注意力缓解了这一成本，使循环次数成为实际的设计选择。因此，我们从收益-成本的角度研究PLT的循环次数选择：额外的循环可能优化表示，但CLP也在每个循环边界引入了位置不匹配。我们通过从头开始在18T token上训练LoopCoder-v2（一组具有不同循环次数的7B PLT代码模型），然后进行匹配的指令微调和评估来实例化这项研究。实证上，两循环变体在代码生成、代码推理、智能体软件工程和工具使用基准测试中，相比无循环基线取得了广泛的增益，将SWE-bench Verified从43.0分提升至64.4分，Multi-SWE从14.0分提升至31.0分。相反，具有三个或更多循环的变体性能下降，揭示了强烈的非单调循环次数效应。我们的诊断表明，循环2提供了主要的生产性优化，而后续循环产生递减的、振荡的更新和降低的表示多样性。由于CLP引起的不匹配大致保持不变，而优化增益减少，偏移成本逐渐占主导。这种收益-成本权衡解释了PLT在两循环时的饱和，并为循环次数选择提供了诊断方法。

Original abstract: Looped Transformers scale latent computation by repeatedly applying shared blocks, but sequential looping increases latency and KV-cache memory with the loop count. Parallel loop Transformers (PLT) alleviate this cost through cross-loop position offsets (CLP) and shared-KV gated sliding-window attention, making loop count a practical design choice. We therefore study PLT loop-count selection through a gain--cost view: an extra loop may refine representations, but CLP also introduces a positional mismatch at each loop boundary. We instantiate this study by training LoopCoder-v2, a family of 7B PLT coders with different loop counts, from scratch on 18T tokens, followed by matched instruction tuning and evaluation. Empirically, the two-loop variant delivers broad gains over the non-looped baseline across code generation, code reasoning, agentic software engineering, and tool-use benchmarks, improving SWE-bench Verified from 43.0 to 64.4 points and Multi-SWE from 14.0 to 31.0 points. In contrast, variants with three or more loops regress, revealing a strongly non-monotonic loop-count effect. Our diagnostics show that loop 2 provides the main productive refinement, while later loops yield diminishing, oscillatory updates and reduced representational diversity. Because the CLP-induced mismatch remains roughly fixed as refinement gains shrink, the offset cost increasingly dominates. This gain--cost trade-off explains PLT's saturation at two loops and provides diagnostics for loop-count selection.

</details>


### [72] [SAE Interventions are Unreliable: Post-Intervention Recovery of Suppressed Behavior](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18322v1)
*Mingyue Cui,Linghui Shen,Xingyi Yang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: SAE干预不可靠研究，揭示agent安全控制失效模式，可迁移至agent鲁棒性

TL;DR: SAE特征干预存在可恢复漏洞，即干预后模型可通过优化恢复原始行为，表明特征控制不等于行为控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究SAE特征干预的可靠性，发现即使在成功干预下，模型行为仍可恢复，暴露了特征级控制与行为完备性之间的差距。

Method: 提出干预后恢复优化问题，从干预后残差状态优化扰动以恢复行为，同时保持目标特征值；使用编码器正交更新和特征映射雅可比矩阵排除撤销干预的可能性。

Result: 在多个实验（TPP、反学习、IOI、拒绝引导）中证实恢复存在；在拒绝引导中恢复率达95.8%，特征相对漂移0.131。

Conclusion: SAE特征控制不能保证对底层行为的控制，存在恢复漏洞。

中文摘要：稀疏自编码器（SAE）将残差流激活分解为可解释的特征。最近的潜在空间防御越来越多地依赖这些分解，假设被识别为“不安全”的SAE特征可以作为监控和干预的可操作句柄。在这种范式下，固定某个特定有害特征预计能可靠地防止模型不当行为。然而，我们表明这种成功可能隐藏了一种可恢复的失败模式：固定可能阻塞了通往某一行为的一条可见路径，但并未消除该行为本身。我们将此漏洞形式化为干预后恢复，这是一个约束残差空间优化问题。从干预后的残差状态开始，我们优化残差扰动以恢复干预前的行为，同时保持目标SAE特征的干预后值。即使在干预在优化和生成过程中始终保持活跃的强威胁模型下，恢复仍然是可能的。为了排除恢复仅仅是撤销干预的可能性，我们在单层干预中使用编码器正交更新，在跨层设置中使用相应的特征映射雅可比矩阵。在TPP、反学习、IOI和拒绝引导实验中，这种压力测试揭示了尽管特征层面干预成功，但仍然存在可恢复的行为。特别是在安全关键的拒绝引导设置中，我们在有效样本上实现了95.8%的恢复率，同时保持被保护特征的相对漂移为0.131，远低于基于后缀的基线。恢复路径归因分析进一步将这种恢复定位到SAE重构残差，即SAE未解释的组件。这些结果揭示了特征层面控制与行为完备性之间的差距：SAE特征可以支持因果干预，但控制它们并不能保证对底层行为的控制。

Original abstract: Sparse Autoencoders (SAEs) decompose residual-stream activations into interpretable features. Recent latent-space defenses increasingly rely on these decompositions, assuming that identified "unsafe" SAE features serve as actionable handles for monitoring and intervention. In this paradigm, clamping a specific harmful feature is expected to reliably prevent model misbehavior. However, we show that this success may hide a recoverable failure mode: the clamp may block one visible route to a behavior without eliminating the behavior itself. We formulate this vulnerability as post-intervention recovery, a constrained residual-space optimization problem. Starting from the post-intervention residual state, we optimize residual perturbations to recover the pre-intervention behavior while preserving the post-intervention values of the targeted SAE features. Even under a strong threat model where the intervention remains active throughout optimization and generation, recovery remains possible. To rule out that recovery simply undoes the intervention, we use encoder-orthogonal updates for single-layer interventions and the corresponding feature-map Jacobian in the cross-layer setting. Across TPP, unlearning, IOI, and refusal steering experiments, this stress test reveals recoverable behavior despite successful feature-level intervention. Especially in the safety-critical refusal-steering setting, we achieve a 95.8% recovery rate on valid samples while keeping defended-feature relative drift to 0.131, substantially below suffix-based baselines. A recovery-path attribution analysis further localizes this recovery to the SAE reconstruction residual, the component left unexplained by the SAE. These results expose a gap between feature-level control and behavioral completeness: SAE features can support causal intervention, but controlling them does not guarantee control over the underlying behavior.

</details>


### [73] [LLMZero: Discovering Adaptive Training Strategies for RL Post-Training via LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18388v1)
*Haoyang Fang,Wei Zhu,Boran Han,Alex Zhang,Zhenyu Pan,Shuo Yang,Shuai Zhang,Jiading Gai,Peng Tang,Cuixiong Hu,Xuan Zhu,Huzefa Rangwala,George Karypis,Bernie Wang*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: LLM agent通过树搜索发现训练策略，通用agent方法可迁移至代码优化超参数搜索。

TL;DR: 通过LLMZero系统发现RL后训练中容量和正则化参数的不同动态模式，提出多阶段训练设计原则，并在多个任务上显著提升性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固定调度无法适应非平稳的探索-利用权衡，需要更好的多阶段训练策略。

Method: 提出LLMZero系统，使用LLM代理通过树搜索搜索训练轨迹，诊断病理并提出多参数协调转换。

Result: 在4个GRPO任务上，相比基础模型提升9%-140%，相比网格搜索提升6%-15%，优于随机搜索和基于技能的代理。

Conclusion: 发现的参数动态模式跨任务转移，解释了不同形式策略的共享动力学，提供了实用设计规则。

中文摘要：RL后训练策略依赖于数据集，并揭示了一个反复出现的经验模式：容量参数在各阶段单调累积，而正则化参数则主要随训练动态变化而振荡。这种区分很重要，因为固定调度将所有参数固定到预定轨迹，因此无法表达正则化必须追踪的非平稳探索-利用权衡；该原理为多阶段训练提供了可操作的设计规则。我们通过LLMZero发现这一点，该系统让LLM代理通过树搜索来搜索训练轨迹，诊断每个检查点的病态并提出协调的多参数转换。在4个不同的GRPO任务中，LLMZero发现的策略相比基础模型相对提升9%到140%，相比网格搜索相对提升6%到15%，始终优于随机搜索和基于技能的代理。该结构原理跨任务迁移，解释了为何发现的策略在形式上定性不同却共享相似的参数动态。

Original abstract: RL post-training strategies are dataset-dependent and reveal a recurring empirical pattern: capacity parameters accumulate monotonically across stages, while regularization parameters predominantly oscillate in response to shifting training dynamics. This distinction matters because fixed schedules commit all parameters to fixed trajectories and therefore cannot express the non-stationary exploration-exploitation tradeoffs that regularization must track; the principle provides actionable design rules for multi-stage training. We discover this through LLMZero, a system where LLM agents search over training trajectories via tree search, diagnosing pathologies at each checkpoint and proposing coordinated multi-parameter transitions. Across 4 diverse GRPO tasks, LLMZero discovers strategies that improve over the base model by 9% to 140% relative and over grid search by 6% to 15% relative, consistently outperforming random search and the skill-based agent. The structural principle transfers across tasks, providing an explanation for why discovered strategies take qualitatively different forms yet share similar parameter dynamics.

</details>


### [74] [SFT Overtraining Predicts Rank Inversion via Entropy Collapse Under RLVR](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18487v2)
*Siddharth Aphale,Kelly Liu*

Main category: cs.LG

Selection reason: 分析RL训练中熵崩溃与排名反转，对agent训练诊断有借鉴价值。

TL;DR: 研究发现，选择 pass@1 最高的 SFT 检查点进行 GRPO 训练可能失败，尤其是在 SFT 过度压缩分布时。提出基于熵的两阶段诊断方法可提前识别高风险检查点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准 GRPO 训练中选择 SFT 检查点的启发式方法（最高 pass@1）可能失效，导致性能退化。需要理解失效机制并设计诊断方法以避免训练浪费。

Method: 在 Qwen2.5-Coder-3B（5深度，3种子）和 DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B（4深度，3种子）上进行实验，测量预 RL pass@1、熵与 GRPO 表现的关系。分析二元奖励下组内方差公式，提出结合预 RL 熵和早期 GRPO 熵的两阶段诊断。

Result: Qwen 上，预 RL pass@1 随深度增加，但 GRPO pass@10 从 0.806 降至 0.481，且预 RL 熵与 GRPO 结果正相关（ρ=+0.69）。DeepSeek 上 pass@1 保持高位，GRPO 表现压缩但未反转。两阶段诊断可识别高风险检查点并提前终止。简单 KL 正则化和标签平滑无法修复 Qwen 的崩溃。

Conclusion: 高 SFT 深度导致低熵分布，使 GRPO 失去组相对信号而失败。两阶段诊断（预 RL 熵 + 早期 GRPO 熵监控）有效预测并防止此类失败，且该失败并非超参数调节可解决。

中文摘要：选择具有最高 pass@1 的 SFT 检查点这一标准启发式方法在 SFT 压缩 rollout 分布时可能失败。对于二元奖励，组内优势方差的期望为 $p(1{-}p)(g{-}1)/g$；当早期 GRPO 将 $p$ 驱动到低于 $p^*(g)$ 时，大多数组具有相同的奖励，从而不提供组相对信号。我们研究了 Qwen2.5-Coder-3B 和 DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B 的 SFT 深度阶梯。我们在五种深度和三个种子上测试了 Qwen2.5-Coder-3B，在四种匹配深度和三个种子上测试了 DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B。在 Qwen 上，预 RL pass@1 随着 SFT 深度增加而上升，但 GRPO pass@10 峰值从 $0.806$ 下降到 $0.481$（3 种子均值，$n{=}20$）；预 RL 熵与 GRPO 结果正相关（$ρ{=}{+}0.69$）。在 DeepSeek 上，pass@1 远高于 $p^*(8){=}0.083$，GRPO 结果压缩而非反转。一种两阶段诊断方法，结合预 RL 熵分类与早期 GRPO 熵监控，可以标记高风险检查点并提前停止失败的运行。在我们的设置中，简单的 KL 参考正则化和标签平滑变体无法挽救崩溃的 Qwen 检查点，这表明该失败并非简单的 GRPO 超参数伪影。

Original abstract: The standard heuristic of selecting the SFT checkpoint with the highest pass@1 for GRPO can fail when SFT compresses the rollout distribution. For binary rewards, the expected within group advantage variance is $p(1{-}p)(g{-}1)/g$; when early GRPO drives $p$ below $p^*(g)$, most groups have identical rewards and provide no group relative signal. We study SFT depth ladders for Qwen2.5-Coder-3B and DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B. We test Qwen2.5-Coder-3B across five depths and three seeds, and DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B across four matched depths and three seeds. On Qwen, pre RL pass@1 rises with SFT depth, but peak GRPO pass@10 falls from $0.806$ to $0.481$ (3 seed mean, $n{=}20$); pre RL entropy is positively associated with the GRPO outcome ($ρ{=}{+}0.69$). On DeepSeek, pass@1 remains far above $p^*(8){=}0.083$, and GRPO outcomes compress rather than invert. A two stage diagnostic, combining pre RL entropy triage with an early GRPO entropy monitor, flags high risk checkpoints and can stop failing runs early. Simple KL to reference regularisation and label smoothing variants do not rescue the collapsed Qwen checkpoint in our setting, suggesting the failure is not a trivial GRPO hyperparameter artefact.

</details>

### [75] [The Consistency Dilemma in LLMs: Generator-Evaluator Agreement and Vulnerability to Mistakes](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30653v1)
*Marina Mancoridis,Zoë Hitzig*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: 研究LLM生成器-评估器自一致性，对agent中自我验证有潜在启发。

TL;DR: 提出生成器-评估器自洽性度量，发现大语言模型存在一致性困境：自洽性高的模型更易犯错误，部署不安全。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验模型在生成和评估输出时是否一致应用概念，这是代理管道可靠性的隐含假设。

Method: 提出生成器-评估器自洽性度量，在10个前沿模型和491个概念上测试，并在临床环境中验证。

Result: 自洽性存在显著差异；在临床环境中，自洽性高的模型与更大的错误脆弱性相关。

Conclusion: 存在一致性困境：自洽性在操作上有用，但更一致的模型也更容易出错，因此不安全。

中文摘要：大语言模型越来越多地部署在代理管道中，这些管道依赖于模型评估自身输出而无需外部验证。这些管道的可靠性依赖于一个隐含假设：模型在生成输出和随后评估该输出时以相同的方式应用相关概念。我们提出了一种新的度量，即生成器-评估器自洽性，以直接测试这一假设，并将其应用于10个前沿模型和491个概念。我们首先发现，自洽性存在显著差异。其次，我们发现在一个临床环境中，经过医生验证的错误（Proniakin等，2025），在模型中，自洽性较高的模型与更大的错误脆弱性相关。因此，即使模型一致地应用概念，它们可能也不安全部署。这是大语言模型中一致性困境的证据：自洽性在操作上有用，但更一致的模型也更容易出错。

Original abstract: Large language models are increasingly deployed in agentic pipelines that depend on the model evaluating its own outputs without external verification. The reliability of these pipelines depends on an implicit assumption: that the model applies relevant concepts the same way when it generates an output and later evaluates that output. We propose a new measure, generator-evaluator self-consistency, to test this assumption directly and apply it to 10 frontier models across 491 concepts. We find, first, that there is substantial variation in self-consistency. Second, we find that in a clinical setting with physician-validated mistakes (Proniakin et al., 2025), across models, those with higher self-consistency are linked to greater vulnerability to mistakes. Thus, even when models consistently apply concepts they may not be safe to deploy. This is evidence of a consistency dilemma in LLMs: self-consistency is operationally useful, but models that are more consistent are also more prone to mistakes.

</details>


### [76] [Agentic AI Enhances Physician Trust in Clinical Decision Making](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.30658v1)
*Zhiling Yan,Zhe Fang,David J King,Ann Pongsakul,Eashan Adhikarla,Hui Ren,Sunyang Fu,Quanzheng Li,Lifang He,Xiang Li,Hongfang Liu,Yonghui Wu,Lichao Sun*

Main category: cs.CY

Selection reason: 医疗agentic AI，研究工具透明与信任，可迁移至agent信任评估

TL;DR: 医生对智能体AI的信任显著高于非智能体模型，尤其在治疗规划任务中，但存在对错误输出的过度依赖，需临床监督。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管智能体AI在医疗中表现优异，但医生对其信任程度尚未被充分研究，本研究旨在量化医生对智能体AI的认知信任和行为依赖。

Method: 三位医生评估315个多模态临床案例，比较智能体AI与非智能体基线，量化过程导向的认知信任和结果导向的行为依赖。

Result: 医生对智能体AI的认知和行为信任显著更高（P<0.001），治疗规划任务中89.57%案例偏好智能体，认知信任与行为依赖显著相关，但存在对错误输出的过度依赖。

Conclusion: 智能体AI能提升医生信任，但决策透明性不足以消除过度依赖，需要持续临床监督。

中文摘要：医疗AI已从推理转向智能体AI，这是一种新范式，能够在推理过程中自主调用外部工具，使中间推理步骤和工具输出对用户透明。尽管已被证明优于先前的模型，但医生对智能体AI的信任仍 largely 未被探索。为解决此问题，三位医生评估了315个多模态临床案例，量化了面向过程的认知信任和面向结果的行为依赖。将智能体AI与非智能体基线进行比较，医生对智能体模型表现出显著更高的认知和行为信任（P < 0.001）。具体而言，在治疗规划任务中，医生最信任智能体推理，在89.57%的案例中倾向于它。此外，面向过程的认知信任与面向结果的行为依赖显著相关（P < 0.001）。然而，对错误智能体输出的可测量过度依赖仍然存在，凸显了仅靠决策逻辑透明度的固有局限，并强调了对严格临床监督的持续需求。

Original abstract: Medical AI has shifted from reasoning to agentic AI, a new paradigm that autonomously invokes external tools during reasoning, rendering intermediate reasoning steps and tool outputs transparent to users. Although proven to outperform previous models, physician trust in agentic AI remains largely unexplored. To address this, three physicians evaluated 315 multimodal clinical cases quantifying both process-oriented cognitive trust and outcome-oriented behavioral reliance. Comparing agentic AI against non-agentic baselines, physicians exhibited significantly higher cognitive and behavioral trust for the agentic model (P < 0.001). Specifically, on treatment planning tasks, physicians trusted the agentic reasoning most, preferring it in 89.57% of cases. Furthermore, process-oriented cognitive trust is significantly associated with outcome-oriented behavioral reliance (P < 0.001). However, measurable over-reliance on incorrect agentic outputs still exists, highlighting the inherent limitations of decision-logic transparency alone and underscoring the continuous need for rigorous clinician oversight.

</details>

### [77] [Querying an astronomical database using large language models: the ALeRCE text-to-SQL system](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18108v1)
*P. A. Estevez,J. Espejo-Moreira,S. Sanfeliu-Alvarez,F. Forster,A. M. Munoz Arancibia,G. Cabrera-Vives,F. E. Bauer,A. Bayo,M. Catelan,R. Dastidar,L. Hernandez-Garcia,J. A. Intriago,G. Pignata*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

Selection reason: LLM驱动的text-to-SQL系统，含模式链接、自我纠正等模块，可视为代码生成agent并借鉴其流水线。

TL;DR: 提出基于LLM的文本到SQL系统，采用逐步生成框架和上下文学习，在ALeRCE天文数据库上表现优于基线。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 使非专业用户能够通过自然语言查询天文数据库，降低使用SQL的门槛。

Method: 构建110对NL/SQL数据集，提出包括模式链接、查询分类、提示分解和自我纠正的逐步生成框架，评估13个LLM。

Result: 逐步框架优于直接推理，自纠正减少错误；Claude Opus 4.6在简单查询上PM达0.97/0.94，困难查询降至0.59/0.49。

Conclusion: 基于LLM的文本到SQL系统有效，逐步方法和自我纠正提升性能，最佳模型为Claude Opus 4.6等。

中文摘要：我们开发了一个基于大型语言模型（LLM）的文本到SQL（结构化查询语言）系统，采用上下文学习技术，并将其应用于自动学习快速事件分类（ALeRCE）天文数据库。ALeRCE是兹威基瞬变设施和维拉·C·鲁宾天文台的社区中介系统。该系统使用户能够以自然语言（NL）查询数据库，并生成可执行的SQL查询。为了开发和评估该系统，我们构建了一个包含110个NL/SQL对的数据集。我们提出了一个逐步生成框架，包含四个模块：模式链接、查询分类、提示分解和自我纠正。我们使用上下文学习和提示工程技术评估了十三个LLM的性能。文本到SQL的性能通过行标识符（如对象标识符）和列标识符（即列名）的完美匹配（PM）率进行评估。所提出的逐步框架始终优于直接推理基线，而自我纠正模块持续减少执行错误。对于Claude Opus 4.6，简单查询的行（列）标识符PM性能很高，达到0.97（0.94），随着查询复杂度增加，中等查询降至0.44（0.72），困难查询降至0.59（0.49）。在评估的十三个模型中，文本到SQL任务中表现最佳的LLM是Claude Opus 4.6、Gemini 2.5 Pro、Gemini 3 Flash和GPT-5.2-Codex。

Original abstract: We develop a text-to-SQL (structured query language) system based on large language models (LLMs) using in-context learning and apply it to the Automatic Learning for the Rapid Classification of Events (ALeRCE) astronomical database. ALeRCE is a community broker for the Zwicky Transient Facility and the Vera C. Rubin Observatory. The system enables users to query the database in natural language (NL) and generates executable SQL queries. To develop and evaluate the system, we constructed a dataset of 110 NL/SQL pairs. We propose a step-by-step generation framework comprising four modules: schema linking, query classification, prompt decomposition, and self-correction. The performance of thirteen LLMs is evaluated using in-context learning and prompt engineering techniques. Text-to-SQL performance is assessed using the perfect-match (PM) rate for row identifiers (e.g., object identifiers) and column identifiers (i.e., column names). The proposed step-by-step framework consistently outperforms a direct-inference baseline, while the self-correction module consistently reduces execution errors. For Claude Opus 4.6, PM performance on row (column) identifiers is high for simple queries, reaching 0.97 (0.94), and decreases with query complexity to 0.44 (0.72) for medium queries and 0.59 (0.49) for hard queries. Among the thirteen evaluated models, the best-performing LLMs for the text-to-SQL task are Claude Opus 4.6, Gemini 2.5 Pro, Gemini 3 Flash, and GPT-5.2-Codex.

### [78] [SoK: AI-Augmented Binary Reversing](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17398v1)
*Yujeong Kwon,Yiyue Zhang,Shakhzod Yuldoshkhujaev,Kexin Pei,Dokyung Song,Hyungjoon Koo*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文系统化梳理了AI增强的二进制逆向工程领域，分析了144篇论文，提出了包含22个领域的分类法和统一框架，揭示了共同结构、技术挑战和未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二进制逆向工程因编译信息丢失而困难，现有AI增强工作碎片化，缺乏系统化知识。

Method: 分析144篇论文，按推理任务分为22个领域，提出统一分类法连接传统与AI增强流程。

Result: 揭示了不同方法间的共同结构、技术挑战和评估差距，识别了未来研究机会。

Conclusion: 提供了领域整体视图和基础，促进下一代可靠可扩展的AI增强二进制逆向系统发展。

中文摘要：二进制逆向工程是软件理解、漏洞发现、恶意软件调查和固件审计的基础。然而，由于编译过程中语义信息的不可逆损失，它仍然具有固有的挑战性。机器学习、大型语言模型（LLM）和智能体AI系统的最新进展加速了AI增强的二进制逆向工程的采用。然而，由此产生的研究工作在不同逆向领域、工件表示、学习方法和评估实践中变得越来越碎片化。本文提出了关于AI增强二进制逆向工程的第一个全面的知识系统化。我们分析了自2015年以来的144篇研究论文，并根据推理任务将其组织成22个二进制逆向领域。我们进一步引入了一个统一的分类法，涵盖了传统和AI增强的逆向流程。我们的分类法连接了传统分析技术、二进制衍生工件、表示策略、学习范式和下游推理任务，同时阐明了LLM和智能体AI系统的新兴角色。通过建立通用词汇和结构化框架，我们提供了对该领域过去十年演变的整体视角。我们的研究揭示了看似不同方法背后的共同结构，突出了持续的技术挑战和评估差距，并指出了未来研究的有希望的机会。总的来说，这些见解阐明了该领域的当前状态，并为下一代可靠且可扩展的AI增强二进制逆向系统奠定了基础。

Original abstract: Binary reversing is fundamental to software understanding, vulnerability discovery, malware investigation, and firmware auditing. However, it remains inherently challenging due to the irreversible loss of semantic information during compilation. Recent advances in machine learning, large language models (LLMs), and agentic AI systems have accelerated the adoption of AI-augmented binary reversing. Yet, the resulting body of work has become increasingly fragmented across reversing domains, artifact representations, learning approaches, and evaluation practices. This paper presents the first comprehensive systematization of knowledge on AI-augmented binary reversing. We analyze 144 research papers published since 2015, and organize them into 22 binary reversing domains according to the inference tasks. We further introduce a unified taxonomy spanning conventional and AI-augmented reversing pipelines. Our taxonomy connects traditional analysis techniques, binary-derived artifacts, representation strategies, learning paradigms, and downstream inference tasks, while clarifying the emerging roles of LLMs and agentic AI systems. By establishing a common vocabulary and structured framework, we provide a holistic view of the field's evolution over the past decade. Our study reveals common structures underlying seemingly disparate approaches, highlights persistent technical challenges and evaluation gaps, and identifies promising opportunities for future research. Collectively, these insights clarify the current state of the field and provide a foundation for the next generation of reliable and scalable AI-augmented binary reversing systems.

### [79] [Structural Role Injection in Handlebars-Templated LLM Prompts: Triple-Brace Interpolation, Delimiter Family, and the Limits of HTML Auto-Escaping](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18120v1)
*Mohammadreza Rashidi*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 研究LLM提示注入风险，直接关系到agent安全设计，对构建可靠编码agent有重要启发。

TL;DR: Handlebars的HTML转义仅能防护特定类型的角色分隔符注入，无法作为通用安全机制，指令与数据需结构分离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究Handlebars默认转义设置在不同角色分隔符下对结构性注入的防护效果差异，揭示其对模型安全性的潜在影响。

Method: 无模型机制分析结合5760次试验，覆盖七种分隔符家族、两种攻击目标及四种模型，评估Handlebars转义对角色注入的防护能力。

Result: GPT-3.5 Turbo在尖括号分隔符家族外仍高度易受攻击，Claude Haiku 4.5则几乎完全抵抗；转义保护仅限于HTML转义覆盖的字符。

Conclusion: Handlebars默认转义无法替代指令与数据的结构分离，仅对部分分隔符有效，需设计更通用的安全方案。

中文摘要：大语言模型应用从模板构建提示，而Handlebars是一种广泛使用的模板引擎，也是Microsoft Semantic Kernel中默认的提示模板格式。其双花括号{x}表达式会对插值进行HTML转义，并被记录为安全默认值；而三花括号{x}表达式则原样插入值。我们表明，这一选择静默地决定了应用程序对结构角色注入的暴露程度，其中攻击者控制的数据携带着能伪造高权限回合的聊天角色分隔符。一项无模型分析揭示了该机制：Handlebars的转义重写了尖括号，但不重写方括号、冒号或Markdown井号，因此它中和了ChatML、Llama-3和XML角色分隔符（存活率0.00），同时保留了Llama-2 [INST]、旧式Human:/Assistant:和Markdown ###分隔符（后两者的存活率为1.00）。随后，我们在七种分隔符家族、两种攻击目标和四种模型（GPT-3.5 Turbo、GPT-4o mini、GPT-4.1 mini、Claude Haiku 4.5）上进行了5760次试验，总API成本为1.63美元。GPT-3.5 Turbo在97%的原始试验和91%的转义试验中遵循了任务劫持指令，其中转义保护集中在尖括号家族，而对冒号和基于Markdown的家族无效；更难的目标（秘密泄露）未达到饱和，更清晰地揭示了相同的家族交互。Claude Haiku 4.5几乎完全抵抗了这两种目标。转义默认值仅保护HTML转义恰好覆盖的分隔符方案，对其他方案不提供保护，并且无法替代指令与数据的结构分离。

Original abstract: Large language model applications build prompts from templates, and Handlebars is a widely used templating engine and the default prompt-template format in Microsoft Semantic Kernel. Its double-brace {x} expression HTML-escapes the interpolated value and is documented as the safe default; its triple-brace {x} expression inserts the value raw. We show that this choice silently governs an application's exposure to structural role injection, where attacker-controlled data carries chat role delimiters that forge a higher-privilege turn. A model-free analysis establishes the mechanism: Handlebars escaping rewrites angle brackets but not square brackets, colons, or Markdown hashes, so it neutralises ChatML, Llama-3, and XML role delimiters (survival rate 0.00) while leaving Llama-2 [INST], legacy Human:/Assistant:, and Markdown ### delimiters intact (survival rate 1.00 for the last two). We then run 5760 trials across seven delimiter families, two attack objectives, and four models (GPT-3.5 Turbo, GPT-4o mini, GPT-4.1 mini, Claude Haiku 4.5) at a combined API cost of 1.63 USD. GPT-3.5 Turbo follows the task-hijack instruction in 97% of raw and 91% of escaped trials, with the escaping protection concentrated in the angle-bracket families and absent for the colon- and Markdown-based families; the harder secret-exfiltration objective, which does not saturate, exposes the same family interaction more cleanly. Claude Haiku 4.5 resists both objectives almost entirely. The escaped default protects only the delimiter schemes whose characters HTML escaping happens to cover, gives no protection for the rest, and cannot substitute for a structural separation of instruction and data.

</details>


### [80] [Agentra: A Supervisable Multi-Agent Framework for Enterprise Intrusion Response](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18325v2)
*Raj Patel,Shaswata Mitra,Michele Guida,Stefano Iannucci,Sudip Mittal,Shahram Rahimi*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 多agent入侵响应框架，含规划-验证循环与审计，可迁移至coding agent

TL;DR: Agentra是一个可监督的多智能体入侵响应框架，通过结构化计划和验证机制，显著提升了响应性能并降低了有害行动率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 静态剧本和分析师驱动的响应方法导致延迟，需要更高效、可审计的自动响应方案。

Method: 采用多智能体框架，角色限定智能体分解推理，规划器-验证器循环验证，审核安全网关筛选威胁情报，行动目录和风险评分门控行动，附加审计日志记录决策。

Result: 在120事件语料上，最强配置的FP感知IRS F1从0.61提升至0.84，有害行动率降至0.0%，而仅有规划器配置会导致不安全过度反应。

Conclusion: 多智能体响应规划能改善基于本体的入侵响应系统覆盖率，同时保留分析师批准和可审计性。

中文摘要：企业入侵响应仍然依赖于静态剧本和分析师驱动的分类，导致从告警生成到响应之间存在延迟。我们提出Agentra，一个可监督的多智能体入侵响应系统（IRS）框架，它将来自IDS、EDR和XDR平台的告警转换为基于MITRE ATT&CK、MITRE D3FEND和NIST CSF 2.0的结构化事件响应计划。Agentra将响应推理分解到角色限定智能体中，通过有界的规划器-验证器审查循环验证提出的计划，通过审核安全网关筛选检索到的威胁情报，通过行动目录和风险评分对行动进行门控，并将决策记录在仅追加的审计日志中。我们评估了Agentra与基于120个事件的语料库（来自ThreatHunter-Playbook、Splunk BOTSv3和DARPA OpTC）的静态OASIS CACAO v2.0网络剧本基线的对比。最强配置将FP感知的IRS F1从0.61提高到0.84，并将预计的有害行动率恢复到静态基线水平0.0%，而仅有规划器的配置引入了不安全的过度反应。这些结果表明，多智能体响应规划可以在保留分析师批准和可审计性的同时，改善基于本体的IRS覆盖率。

Original abstract: Enterprise intrusion response still depends on static playbooks and analyst-driven triage, creating delay between alert generation and containment. We present Agentra, a supervisable multi-agent Intrusion Response System (IRS) framework that converts alerts from IDS, EDR, and XDR platforms into structured incident response plans grounded in MITRE ATT&CK, MITRE D3FEND, and NIST CSF 2.0. Agentra decomposes response reasoning across role-scoped agents, validates proposed plans through a bounded Planner--Validator review loop, screens retrieved threat intelligence through a Moderator security gateway, gates actions through an Action Catalog and risk score, and records decisions in an append-only audit log. We evaluate Agentra against a static OASIS CACAO v2.0 cyber-playbook baseline on a 120-event corpus drawn from ThreatHunter-Playbook, Splunk BOTSv3, and DARPA OpTC. The strongest configuration improves FP-aware IRS F1 from 0.61 to 0.84 and restores the projected harmful-action rate to the static baseline level of 0.0% after Planner-only configurations introduce unsafe overreaction. These results indicate that multi-agent response planning can improve ontology-grounded IRS coverage while preserving analyst approval and auditability.

### [81] [A Red-Team Study of Anthropic Fable 5 & Opus 4.8 Models](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18193v1)
*Nicola Franco*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 红队攻击框架，涉及agent自动对抗生成与安全性，可迁移至agent安全控制

TL;DR: 评估了两个前沿LLM对抗自动化越狱攻击的鲁棒性，发现即使最好的模型在自适应迭代攻击下仍可被攻破，产生大量有害输出。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估前沿LLM的对抗鲁棒性，尤其是针对自动化越狱攻击的表现，以了解当前模型的防御水平。

Method: 使用HackAgent红队框架生成数十万次对抗性尝试，覆盖7,826个有害意图和十类伤害，采用三种评判模型多数投票确认成功。

Result: Opus 4.8在最强自适应攻击下11.5%意图被攻破，Fable 5为6.1%；两模型分别产生1,620和702个专家组确认的有害完成，覆盖所有类别。

Conclusion: 即使最先进、最充分测试的前沿模型，在持续自动压力下仍可靠地被攻破。

中文摘要：我们评估了Anthropic开发的两个前沿大语言模型（LLM）——Fable 5和Opus 4.8——针对四类自动化越狱攻击的对抗鲁棒性，这些攻击覆盖了7,826个有害意图，横跨十个类别的人体分类学。使用HackAgent红队框架，生成了数十万次对抗性尝试，并且每个表面上的成功都由三个评判模型组成的专家组（多数投票）独立重新裁决。两个模型都抵抗了大多数攻击，但剩余攻击面比总体框架所暗示的要大：它主要由自适应迭代攻击主导，而静态混淆几乎被完全消除。最强的自适应搜索（攻击树）在总体意图上对Opus 4.8的攻击成功率为11.5%，而Fable 5保持在个位数（最坏情况6.1%）。因此，总体成功率不应被视为令人放心。即使在这些加固配置中，两个模型也产生了1,620（Opus 4.8）和702（Fable 5）个经专家组确认的有害完成，涵盖了每个有害类别，这些完成是自动、廉价地定位的，并且由攻击模型在没有人类专家参与的情况下在前一两个优化步骤内完成。合理的结论是，即使是最好的、经过最充分测试的前沿模型，在持续自动压力下仍然可以被可靠地攻破。

Original abstract: We evaluate the adversarial robustness of two frontier large language models (LLMs) developed by Anthropic, Fable 5 and Opus 4.8, against four families of automated jailbreak attack across 7 826 harmful intents spanning a ten-category harm taxonomy. Using the HackAgent red-teaming framework, hundreds of thousands of adversarial attempts were generated and every apparent success was independently re-adjudicated by a panel of three judge models (majority vote). Both models resist the majority of attacks, but the residual surface is larger than aggregate framing suggests: it is dominated by adaptive iterative attacks, while static obfuscation is near-fully neutralised. The strongest adaptive search (tree-of-attacks) breaks Opus 4.8 on 11.5% of intents overall, whereas Fable 5 stays in the single digits (6.1% worst-case). Aggregate rates therefore should not be read as reassurance. Even in these hardened configurations, the two models produced 1 620 (Opus 4.8) and 702 (Fable 5) panel-confirmed harmful completions spanning every harm category, located automatically, cheaply, and within the first one or two refinement steps by an attacker model with no human expert in the loop. The reasonable conclusion is that even the best, most-tested frontier models remain reliably breakable under sustained automated pressure.

### [82] [Learning Red Agent Policy from Observations for Neurosymbolic Autonomous Cyber Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18223v2)
*Ankita Samaddar,Sandeep Neema,Daniel Balasubramanian,Xenofon Koutsoukos*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出一种基于模仿学习的策略学习技术，用于在部分可观测的自主网络环境中预测红方代理的动作，辅助神经符号防御代理实现高精度预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自主网络防御中，红方代理的动作不可观测，导致防御者难以预测其行为、学习其策略或评估入侵级别。

Method: 使用模仿学习为离散状态和离散动作的部分可观测RL代理学习策略，从网络观测和防御者动作中预测红方动作，并与神经符号防御代理集成。

Result: 有效处理不同红方策略，并在多种模拟场景中实现高预测精度。

Conclusion: 该方法能够有效提升自主网络防御代理对红方行为的预测能力。

中文摘要：随着复杂网络攻击日益普遍，现代网络需要经过强化学习（RL）训练的智能自主网络防御代理。这些代理采用神经符号方法（如具有学习增强组件（LEC）的行为树）来学习、推理、适应和执行安全规则，同时维持关键操作。然而，这些自主网络是部分可观测系统，即网络攻击者（红方代理）的动作不可观测，这使得防御者难以预测红方动作、学习红方策略或评估攻击者的入侵级别。为了解决这个问题，我们提出了一种使用模仿学习的策略学习技术，用于学习离散状态和离散动作的部分可观测RL代理的策略。我们将该技术应用于自主网络环境，从网络观测和防御者动作中预测红方代理的动作。与神经符号网络防御代理集成，我们的方法有效处理不同的红方策略，并在各种模拟场景中实现高预测精度。

Original abstract: With sophisticated cyber-attacks becoming increasingly prevalent, modern networks require intelligent autonomous cyber-defense agents trained via Reinforcement Learning (RL). These agents employ neurosymbolic approaches such as behavior trees with learning-enabled components (LECs) to learn, reason, adapt, and implement security rules while maintaining critical operations. However, these autonomous networks are partially observable systems, i.e., the cyber-attacker's (red agent's) actions are not observable, making it difficult for the defender to predict red actions, learn red policies, or assess the attacker's intrusion levels. To address this, we propose a Policy Learning Technique using imitation learning to learn policies for partially observable RL agents with discrete states and discrete actions. We apply this technique in an autonomous cyber environment to predict red agent's actions from network observations and defender actions. Integrated with a neurosymbolic cyber-defense agent, our method effectively handles different red policies and achieves high prediction accuracy across diverse simulated scenarios.

### [83] [SafeClawBench: Separating Semantic, Audit-Evidence, and Sandbox Harm in Tool-Using LLM Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18356v1)
*Yuchuan Tian,Mengyu Zheng,Haocheng Mei,Ye Yuan,Chao Xu,Xinghao Chen,Hanting Chen,Yu Wang*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 工具使用agent安全基准，区分多级危害，可迁移至agent安全评测

TL;DR: 提出了SafeClawBench，一个针对使用工具的代理安全的分阶段基准测试，区分语义同意和实际危害。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有评估将不同安全失败阶段合并为单一成功率，难以区分模型是仅同意攻击还是产生了实际可观察危害。

Method: 构建包含600个对抗任务的基准，覆盖六个攻击家族，报告三个端点（语义接受、审计证据、沙箱危害），并在四个提示策略下评估五个代理端点。

Result: 语义失败率在9.0%至44.2%之间；审计证据比语义失败更窄；在12000行匹配分析中，347个沙箱危害中有291个发生在通过语义检查的行中；提示策略的影响因模型和协议而异。

Conclusion: SafeClawBench提供了一个可复现的框架，用于比较代理模型和提示策略条件，避免混淆文本合规性、证据支持的危害和可执行状态变化。

中文摘要：使用工具的语言模型代理引入了超出不安全文本的安全失败：它们可以泄露受保护的对象、写入持久内存、发送消息、修改数据库或触发有害代码和工具效果。现有的评估通常将这些阶段合并为一个攻击成功率，这使得很难区分模型只是同意了攻击者还是实际产生了可观察到的危害。我们引入了SafeClawBench，一个针对使用工具的代理安全的分阶段基准测试，包含600个受控对抗任务，涵盖六个攻击家族：直接和间接提示注入、工具返回注入、内存投毒、内存提取和歧义驱动的不安全推理。SafeClawBench报告三个独立的端点：语义攻击接受、审计可见的危害证据以及沙箱观察到的工具/状态危害。在四个提示级策略下评估五个代理端点，我们发现这些端点捕捉到了不同的失败模式。在没有额外提示保护的情况下，语义失败率在不同模型之间差异很大，从9.0%到44.2%。审计危害证据比语义失败更窄，在一个单独的可执行协议下，一些匹配的任务身份会产生沙箱危害，尽管通过了语义核心调用：在一项12,000行的匹配分析中，347个观察到的沙箱危害中有291个出现在通过语义检查的行中。提示策略会改变端点结果，但其效果取决于模型和协议。SafeClawBench提供了一个可复现的框架，用于比较代理模型和提示策略条件，而不会混淆文本合规性、证据支持的危害和可执行状态变化。开源数据集可在https://huggingface.co/datasets/sairights/safeclawbench获取。

Original abstract: Tool-using language-model agents introduce security failures that go beyond unsafe text: they can disclose protected objects, write persistent memory, send messages, modify databases, or trigger harmful code and tool effects. Existing evaluations often collapse these stages into a single attack success rate, making it difficult to tell whether a model merely agreed with an attacker or actually produced observable harm. We introduce SafeClawBench, a staged benchmark for tool-using agent security with 600 controlled adversarial tasks across six attack families: direct and indirect prompt injection, tool-return injection, memory poisoning, memory extraction, and ambiguity-driven unsafe inference. SafeClawBench reports three separate endpoints: semantic attack acceptance, audit-visible harm evidence, and sandbox-observed tool/state harm. Evaluating five agent endpoints under four prompt-level policies, we find that these endpoints capture different failure modes. Without additional prompt protection, semantic failure rates vary widely across models, from 9.0% to 44.2%. Audited harm evidence is narrower than semantic failure, and under a separate executable protocol some matched task identities produce sandbox harm despite passing the Semantic Core call: in a 12,000-row matched analysis, 291 of 347 observed sandbox harms occur in rows that pass the semantic check. Prompt policies change endpoint outcomes, but their effects depend on both model and protocol. SafeClawBench provides a reproducible framework for comparing agent models and prompt-policy conditions without conflating textual compliance, evidence-supported harm, and executable state changes. The open-source dataset is available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/sairights/safeclawbench.

</details>


### [84] [Ghost Vectors: Soft-Deleted Embeddings Remain Reconstructible in HNSW Vector Databases](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18497v1)
*Chandranil Chakraborttii,Jackeline García Alvarado,Sitora Abdulofizova,Shivanshu Dwivedi*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: 揭示向量数据库软删除漏洞，对agent的RAG安全有启发。

TL;DR: RAG系统中HNSW向量数据库的软删除导致嵌入可被物理恢复，本研究提出纪元密钥轮换方法，通过加密并丢弃密钥实现安全删除，同时生成可审计的删除证明。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RAG系统中HNSW向量数据库的软删除操作未能物理清除数据，导致已删除的嵌入仍可被恢复，违反GDPR和HIPAA等数据擦除法规，存在隐私泄露风险。

Method: 提出纪元密钥轮换（Epoch Key Rotation），对向量进行加密，删除时丢弃加密密钥；同时生成ECDSA签名的加密证明作为删除事件的审计记录。

Result: 在多个数据集上，软删除的嵌入可被高精度恢复；而纪元密钥轮换将PII恢复率降至0%，处理500个向量仅需2.5毫秒。

Conclusion: 纪元密钥轮换能有效防止向量恢复，提供合规的删除机制，且性能开销极低，适合实际部署。

中文摘要：检索增强生成（RAG）允许大语言模型访问外部和私有语料库以生成事实性、领域特定的响应。现代RAG流水线使用分层可导航小世界（HNSW）向量数据库进行高效相似性搜索。当用户请求数据删除时，系统通常仅标记记录为已删除，而将嵌入在磁盘上物理保留。这种软删除操作引发了数据擦除和保留要求（如GDPR第17条和HIPAA）下的合规性问题。对三种HNSW实现的分析证实，通过访问存储层的原始索引文件（绕过API访问），删除的向量在物理上仍然可恢复。使用无需领域特定微调的Vec2Text反转模型，我们在多个真实世界数据集和数据模态上展示了这一漏洞。在维基百科生物人物数据集（BLP）上，我们成功恢复了25.5%的准确人名和46.4%的地理位置（ROUGE-L 0.185）。在高度结构化、敏感数据（NIH Synthea数据集）上，患者年龄和性别标记的恢复率达到100%（ROUGE-L 0.290）。在软删除的图像嵌入上，我们在组织病理学切片上展示了100%的组织分类（p=1.02e-07），面部嵌入的top-1身份恢复达到99%（p<0.01）。本文引入了纪元密钥轮换（Epoch Key Rotation），对向量进行加密并在删除时丢弃密钥。纪元密钥轮换将观察到的PII恢复率降低至0%，并且在500个删除向量上完成时间为2.5毫秒（约0.005毫秒/记录）。此外，它生成一个ECDSA签名的加密证明，作为删除事件的可审计记录。

Original abstract: Retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) allows large language models to access external and private corpora for factual, domain-specific responses. Modern RAG pipelines use hierarchical navigable small world (HNSW) vector databases for efficient similarity search. When a user requests data deletion, the systems typically only mark the record as deleted, leaving the embedding on disk physically unchanged. This soft-delete operation raises compliance concerns under data-erasure and retention requirements such as GDPR Article 17 and HIPAA. Analysis on three HNSW implementations confirms that deleted vectors remain physically recoverable by accessing the raw index files at the storage layer, bypassing API access. Using the Vec2Text inversion model without domain-specific fine-tuning, we show this vulnerability on multiple real-world datasets and data modalities. On Wikipedia biographical living persons dataset (BLP), we successfully recover 25.5% of exact person names and 46.4% of geographic locations (ROUGE-L 0.185). Recovery reaches 100% for both patient age and gender markers (ROUGE-L 0.290) on highly structured, sensitive data (NIH Synthea dataset). On soft-deleted image embeddings, we show 100% tissue classification on histopathology patches (p=1.02e-07) and top-1 identity recovery reaches 99% on facial embeddings (p<0.01). This work introduces Epoch Key Rotation, which encrypts vectors and discards the key upon deletion. Epoch key rotation reduces observed PII recovery to 0% and completes in 2.5 ms for 500 deleted vectors (approximately 0.005 ms/record). Additionally, it generates an ECDSA-signed cryptographic proof as an auditable record of the deletion event.

</details>


### [85] [AI Sandboxes: A Threat Model, Taxonomy, and Measurement Framework](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18532v1)
*Inderjeet Singh,Haitham Mahmoud,Andrés Murillo*

Main category: cs.CR

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 本文形式化了AI沙箱的边界和证据组合规则，提出了沙箱原型分类和威胁模型，并引入了一个测量框架来明确沙箱的测试能力和保证作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着AI系统在物理世界中的部署增加，需要受控环境进行安全评估，但现有沙箱概念缺乏形式化定义和保证框架。

Method: 通过形式化沙箱边界、最弱链路规则、沙箱原型分类、网络物理威胁模型以及包含多维度工件的测量框架，并结合三个案例研究。

Result: 提出了一个威胁模型、分类法和测量框架，阐明了沙箱的有效测试范围、可包含的风险以及支持安全、安保和监管保证的证据类型。

Conclusion: 该框架帮助理解沙箱在AI系统保证中的角色，并为设计和评估沙箱提供指导。

中文摘要：AI系统越来越多地在有界环境中进行评估，这些环境结合了隔离、仿真、仪器、监督和证据捕获。对于物理AI、AIoT和网络物理系统，这种转变不仅仅是术语问题：被测系统可能通过物理过程、网络设备和人类操作员进行感知、决策、执行、通信和故障。本文提出了一种面向保证的AI沙箱描述，将其作为在数字AI、具身自主和网络物理部署中进行测试、评估、验证和确认的受控环境。我们形式化了沙箱边界和一条最弱链路规则，用于将各维度的证据组合成一个有界部署声明；区分了主要的沙箱原型；定义了一个网络物理威胁模型，包括对保证装置本身的攻击；并引入了一个跨越保真度、可控性、可观察性、包容性、可重复性和治理工件的测量框架，通过三个实际沙箱的工作案例进行实例化。由此产生的威胁模型、分类法和测量框架阐明了沙箱可以有效测试的内容、它可以包含的风险以及它支持安全、安保和监管保证的证据形式。

Original abstract: AI systems are increasingly evaluated in bounded environments that combine isolation, simulation, instrumentation, supervision, and evidence capture. For physical AI, AIoT, and cyber-physical systems, this shift is not a matter of terminology: the system under test may sense, decide, actuate, communicate, and fail through physical processes, networked devices, and human operators. This article develops an assurance-oriented account of AI sandboxes as controlled environments for testing, evaluation, verification, and validation across digital AI, embodied autonomy, and cyber-physical deployments. We formalize the sandbox boundary and a weakest-link rule for composing per-dimension evidence into a bounded deployment claim; separate major sandbox archetypes; define a cyber-physical threat model that includes attacks on the assurance apparatus itself; and introduce a measurement framework spanning fidelity, controllability, observability, containment, reproducibility, and governance artifacts, instantiated on three worked case studies of real sandboxes. The resulting threat model, taxonomy, and measurement framework clarify what a sandbox can validly test, which risks it can contain, and what forms of evidence it can support for safety, security, and regulatory assurance.

### [86] [Verifying the Rust Standard Library](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17374v1)
*Byron Cook,Remi Delmas,Zyad Hassan,Bart Jacobs,Ranjit Jhala,Rahul Kumar,Felipe R. Monteiro,Thanh Nguyen,Rebecca Rumbul,Michael Tautschnig,Celina Val,Carolyn Zech*

Main category: cs.LO

Selection reason: cs.SE 论文按全量策略收录。

TL;DR: 通过众包方式将多种验证工具集成到Rust标准库分支的持续集成中，开展了迄今为止最大的软件库验证活动，分析了有效性和实际价值，并提出未解决挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Rust标准库大量依赖unsafe代码，目前仅通过动态测试验证，缺乏静态验证，存在内存错误风险。

Method: 发起开放、众包的活动，将互补的验证工具集成到从Rust标准库分支的验证仓库的持续集成中。

Result: 完成了大规模验证活动，分析了其有效性，并证明了机器检查证明对部分未定义行为的实际价值。

Conclusion: 该验证活动有效，但仍有障碍需形式化方法社区进一步解决。

中文摘要：Rust的类型系统防止了许多类内存错误，但其标准库严重依赖unsafe代码，这些代码的正确性通过测试（包括在Miri下的动态检查）来验证，但缺乏静态验证。我们提出了据我们所知最大的针对软件库的验证活动：一项开放、众包的努力，将互补的验证工具集成到从Rust标准库分支出来的验证仓库的持续集成中。我们分析了该活动的有效性，讨论了机器检查证明对于部分未定义行为（例如越界访问、空指针和悬空指针解引用以及使用未初始化内存）的实际价值，并将剩余的障碍作为形式化方法社区的开放挑战。

Original abstract: Rust's type system prevents many classes of memory errors, yet its standard library relies heavily on unsafe code whose correctness is validated through testing, including dynamic checks under Miri, but lacks static verification. We present what is, to the best of our knowledge, the largest verification campaign reported for a software library: an open, crowdsourced effort that integrates complementary verification tools into the continuous integration of a verification repository forked from the Rust standard library. We analyze the campaign's effectiveness, discuss the practical value of machine-checked proofs for a subset of undefined behaviors (e.g., out-of-bounds access, null and dangling pointer dereferences, and use of uninitialized memory), and frame the remaining obstacles as open challenges for the formal-methods community.

### [87] [AUTOGATE: Automated Clock Gating via Toggling-Aware LLM-based RTL Rewriting](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17461v1)
*Yiting Wang,Chenhui Deng,Chia-Tung Ho,Yanqing Zhang,Zhuo Feng,Cunxi Yu,Ang Li,Gang Qu,Brucek Khailany*

Main category: cs.AR

Selection reason: LLM agent自动优化RTL时钟门控，直接进行代码性能优化，高度相关。

TL;DR: 提出AUTOGATE，首个基于ML-LLM协同的智能体框架，通过层次化多智能体架构和聚类算法实现工业级RTL时钟门控优化，显著降低动态功耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有FGCG优化依赖手动，LLM方法无法处理长波形和大型层次化代码库，缺乏可扩展性和自动化。

Method: ML-LLM协同设计：ML聚类算法将原始波形轨迹提炼为紧凑结构化表示引导LLM重写；层次化多智能体架构将大型设计分解为独立优化模块。

Result: 小型设计平均动态功耗降低49.31%；工业级设计NVDLA降低19.34%，BlackParrot降低7.96%，专有生产设计最高降低6.86%。

Conclusion: AUTOGATE是一种有效的工业级RTL功耗优化框架，实现了自动化、可扩展且工作负载感知的时钟门控优化。

中文摘要：细粒度时钟门控（FGCG）是降低动态功耗最有效的技术之一，然而当前的FGCG优化流程仍然很大程度上依赖手动操作。近期基于LLM的RTL优化方法仍然存在两个主要缺点：(1)无法处理跨越数百万个周期的长波形轨迹，(2)难以在保持正确性的同时将优化扩展到大型层次化代码库。在这项工作中，我们提出了AUTOGATE，首个面向工业级RTL功耗优化的智能体框架，能够在大型层次化代码库中实现工作负载感知的时钟门控优化。AUTOGATE引入了一种机器学习（ML）-LLM协同设计，桥接了波形级分析和RTL重写。具体来说，我们设计了一种基于ML的聚类算法，将原始翻转轨迹提炼为紧凑、结构化的表示，指导基于LLM的RTL重写。这使得能够准确识别和应用时钟门控机会，而无需LLM直接处理原始波形数据。为增强可扩展性，AUTOGATE采用层次化多智能体架构，将大型设计分解为可独立优化的模块，从而在深层设计层次中实现协调优化。我们在从小型RTL设计到大型工业级代码库的多样化设计上评估了AUTOGATE。实验结果表明，AUTOGATE相对于基线持续降低动态功耗。在小型设计套件上，AUTOGATE平均降低动态功耗49.31%。在工业级设计上，AUTOGATE在NVDLA和BlackParrot上分别实现了19.34%和7.96%的动态功耗降低，在高度优化的专有生产设计上最高降低6.86%。

Original abstract: Fine-grain clock gating (FGCG) is among the most effective techniques for reducing dynamic power, yet current FGCG optimization flows remain largely manual. Recent LLM-based RTL optimization approaches remain limited by two key drawbacks: (1) the inability to process long waveform traces spanning millions of cycles, and (2) the difficulty of scaling optimization to large hierarchical codebases while preserving correctness. In this work, we present AUTOGATE, the first agentic framework for industry-grade RTL power optimization, enabling workload-aware clock-gating optimization across large hierarchical codebases. AUTOGATE introduces a Machine Learning (ML)-LLM co-design that bridges waveform-level analysis and RTL rewriting. Specifically, we design an ML-based clustering algorithm that distills raw toggling traces into compact, structured representations that guide LLM-based RTL rewriting. This enables accurate identification and application of clock-gating opportunities without requiring LLMs to directly process raw waveform data. To enhance scalability, AUTOGATE employs a hierarchical multi-agent architecture that decomposes large designs into independently optimizable modules, enabling coordinated optimization across deep design hierarchies. We evaluate AUTOGATE on a diverse set of designs ranging from small RTL designs to large industrial-grade codebases. Experimental results show that AUTOGATE consistently reduces dynamic power relative to baselines. Across the small-design suite, AUTOGATE reduces dynamic power by 49.31% on average. On industry-scale designs, it achieves 19.34% and 7.96% dynamic power reductions on NVDLA and BlackParrot, respectively, and up to 6.86% on highly optimized proprietary production designs.

### [88] [MagicSim: A Unified Infrastructure for Executable Embodied Interaction](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17511v1)
*Haoran Lu,Songling Liu,Yue Chen,Guo Ye,Mutian Shen,Shuyang Yu,Yu Xiao,Jihai Zhao,Shang Wu,Jianshu Zhang,Xiangtian Gui,Chuye Hong,Yuran Wang,Maojiang Su,Jiayi Wang,Ruihai Wu,Zhaoran Wang,Han Liu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

中文摘要：机器人学习和具身智能体现在需要仿真作为一个共享的执行基底，连接控制、技能和规划，而不仅仅是作为渲染器、控制器测试台或固定任务环境。现有的流水线通过“魔法”动作、脱节的训练环境或只能前向渲染且无法重现、评估和标注同一回合的方式将这些层分开。我们提出了MagicSim，一个围绕确定性批处理运行时和共享马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）构建的具身交互基础设施。通过YAML优先的规范，解耦内容、放置、行为和智能体暴露，MagicSim在单次重置-步骤循环中构建了多样化的可执行世界，涵盖任务家族、交互模式、物理、布局、传感器、化身和机器人形态。一个通用的执行接口通过控制器、原子技能、规划器原语和异步规划将高级命令落地，实现为机器人动作而非模拟器端的状态编辑。一个任务定义支持三种能力：基准测试和强化学习评估、自动收集接口（自动将命令转化为接地轨迹）、以及面向智能体/VLM的交互。对于自动执行，命令通过Command->Skill->Planner->Robot->Record流水线流动，而每个环境的命令、技能、规划、重试、标注和回合状态在共享物理滴答之上独立推进。成功的轨迹被保存为结构化的多模态轨迹，将语言监督、动作表示、视觉/几何表示和任务级状态与执行的回合对齐。因此，MagicSim在一个规划器在环的运行时中统一了多样化世界构建、具身执行、任务评估、自动轨迹生成和交互式智能体接口。

Original abstract: Robot learning and embodied agents now require simulation to serve as a shared execution substrate linking control, skills, and planning, not only as a renderer, controller testbed, or fixed task environment. Existing pipelines split these layers with "magic" actions, disconnected training environments, or forward-only renders that cannot reproduce, evaluate, and annotate the same episode. We present MagicSim, an embodied interaction infrastructure built around one deterministic batched runtime and a shared Markov decision process (MDP). From YAML-first specifications that decouple contents, placement, behavior, and agent exposure, MagicSim constructs diverse executable worlds spanning task families, interaction regimes, physics, layouts, sensors, avatars, and robot embodiments in one reset-and-step loop. A common execution interface grounds high-level commands through controllers, atomicskills, planner primitives, and asynchronous planning, realizing them as robot actions rather than simulator-side state edits. One task definition supports three capabilities: benchmark and RL evaluation, an autocollect interface that automatically turns commands into grounded trajectories, and agent/VLM-facing interaction. For automatic execution, commands flow through a Command->Skill->Planner->Robot->Record pipeline, while per-environment command, skill, planning, retry, annotation, and episode states advance independently above the shared physics tick. Successful rollouts are saved as structured multimodal trajectories aligning language supervision, action representations, visual/geometric representations, and task-level status with the executed episode. MagicSim thus unifies diverse world construction, embodied execution, task evaluation, automatic rollout generation, and interactive agent interfaces in one planner-in-the-loop runtime.

### [89] [ED3R: Energy-Aware Distributed Disaster Detection Enabled by Cooperative Robotic Agents](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17739v1)
*Lina Magoula,Nikolaos Koursioumpas,Nancy Alonistioti,Ramin Khalili*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 分布式协作agent框架，含前瞻与能源优化，通用方法可迁移

TL;DR: ED3R是一种能源感知分布式框架，通过分层协作决策和前瞻能力，在不确定性下高效检测野火，显著降低能耗并提高检测速度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在野火等关键任务中，机器人需要在不确定性、资源限制和严格约束下做出决策，同时管理能量消耗和检测时间，现有方法未能充分解决这些挑战。

Method: ED3R框架采用机器人与远程控制器之间的分层协作决策，集成障碍物避免、冗余探索防止、自适应提前完成和自定义惩罚函数，并利用分布式神经回归模型实现前瞻能力。

Result: 在逼真模拟中，ED3R实现了高达97.18%的任务成功率，在最苛刻任务中能耗降低36.4%，检测速度加快41%。

Conclusion: ED3R框架有效提升了野火检测的能源效率和速度，为分布式机器人系统在环境监测和灾害管理中的应用提供了可行方案。

中文摘要：机器人技术有望支持环境监测和自然灾害管理，在此类任务中，决策必须在不确定性、资源限制和严格操作约束下做出。在关键任务（如野火）中，机器人代理不仅需要以足够的置信度识别危险事件，还需要管理能量消耗和检测时间。本文介绍了ED3R，一种面向不确定性下野火检测的能源感知分布式框架。ED3R实现了机器人与远程控制器之间的分层协作决策。远程控制器决定机器人的运动，而机器人感知环境并决定在哪里执行野火检测（机载或远程）以及如何执行。共同目标是以所需置信度检测野火，同时最小化任何机器人操作消耗的能量。ED3R进一步集成了避免附近障碍物、防止冗余探索、实现自适应提前任务完成以及通过自定义惩罚函数确保可行性的机制。ED3R还引入了前瞻能力，该能力通过分布式神经回归模型实现，使代理能够在执行前评估候选策略来预测未来。该框架通过逼真的机器人模拟、消融研究和基线比较进行评估。总体而言，ED3R实现了高达97.18%的任务成功率。特别是在最苛刻的任务中，它比基线减少了高达36.4%的能量消耗，并加快了高达41%的野火检测速度。

Original abstract: Robotics are expected to support environmental monitoring and natural disaster management, where decisions must be made under uncertainty, resource limitations, and strict operational constraints. In critical missions, such as wildfires, robotic agents must not only identify hazardous events with sufficient confidence, but also manage the energy cost and time until detection. This paper introduces ED3R, an energy-aware distributed framework for wildfire detection under uncertainty. ED3R enables hierarchical cooperative decision-making between a robot and a remote controller. The remote controller decides upon the robot's motion, while the robot senses the environment and decides where to execute the wildfire detection (onboard or remotely) and how. The common goal is to detect wildfires with a required confidence while minimizing the energy consumed by any robot operation. ED3R further integrates mechanisms to avoid nearby obstacles, prevent redundant exploration, enable adaptive early mission completion, and ensure feasibility through a custom penalty function. ED3R also introduces a forward-looking capability, enabled through distributed neural regression models that allow the agents to anticipate the future by evaluating candidate strategies before execution. The framework is evaluated through realistic robotics simulations, ablation studies, and baseline comparisons. Overall, ED3R achieves a mission success rate of up to 97.18%. Especially in the most demanding missions, it reduces energy consumption by up to 36.4% and detects wildfires up to 41% faster than baselines.

</details>


### [90] [PearlVLA: Progressive Embodied Action-Plan Refinement in Latent Space](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.17924v1)
*Bochen Yang,Lianlei Shan*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: VLA框架中潜空间计划精炼，可迁移至agent规划与自改进。

TL;DR: PearlVLA通过在VLM的潜在空间中进行迭代规划精炼，结合未来引导的残差更新和因果强化学习，实现了高效且性能领先的视觉-语言-动作控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型在快速动作生成与显式规划推理之间存在矛盾，直接解码速度虽快但规划能力弱，而显式推理则带来高延迟和计算开销，因此需要一种在潜在空间中进行高效推理的方法。

Method: 提出PearlVLA框架，将VLM的元查询分为视觉接地分支和潜在规划分支；通过计划条件世界查询从轻量级潜在世界模型获取未来观测潜在表示，并由未来引导的RefineNet进行多轮残差更新精炼规划；采用因果精炼分组过程奖励强化学习优化精炼过程。

Result: 在LIBERO基准上，PearlVLA达到了现有方法中最先进的性能。

Conclusion: 通过将推理转移到潜在空间并结合迭代精炼与强化学习，PearlVLA实现了高效且高性能的动作规划，为VLA模型的设计提供了新范式。

中文摘要：当前的视觉-语言-动作（VLA）模型在高效动作生成与显式推理之间面临权衡。直接从视觉-语言骨干表示中解码动作能够实现低延迟控制，而通过文本链、像素级子目标或动作搜索进行显式推理可以改善规划，但会带来大量的延迟和计算成本。我们提出了PearlVLA，一种将推理转移到视觉-语言模型（VLM）潜在空间中的VLA框架。PearlVLA将VLM的元查询表示分为一个固定的视觉接地分支和一个迭代的潜在规划分支。在每个精炼轮次中，一个以规划为条件的世界查询会探测一个轻量级冻结的潜在世界模型，以获得一个无动作的未来观测潜在表示，该表示被反馈回来指导规划的改进。一个未来引导的RefineNet随后应用预定的残差更新，逐步将粗糙的语义草稿改进为细粒度的潜在动作规划。经过K轮改进后的规划被并行解码为一个动作块，以实现低延迟执行。我们进一步引入了因果精炼分组过程奖励强化学习，以优化潜在精炼过程，其奖励来自由潜在规划编辑引发的更长视野想象中的未来。在LIBERO基准上的实证评估表明，PearlVLA在现有方法中达到了最先进的性能。

Original abstract: Current Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models face a trade-off between efficient action generation and explicit deliberation. Directly decoding actions from vision-language backbone representations enables low-latency control, whereas explicit reasoning through textual chains, pixel-level subgoals, or action search can improve planning but incurs substantial latency and computational cost. We propose PearlVLA, a VLA framework that moves deliberation into the latent space of a vision-language model (VLM). PearlVLA separates VLM meta-query representations into a fixed visual grounding branch and an iterative latent plan branch. At each refinement round, a plan-conditioned world query probes a lightweight frozen latent world model for an action-free future observation latent, which is fed back to guide plan refinement. A future-guided RefineNet then applies scheduled residual updates to progressively refine a coarse semantic draft into a fine-grained latent action plan. The refined plan after K rounds is then decoded in parallel into an action chunk for low-latency execution. We further introduce Causal Refinement-Grouped Process-Reward RL to optimize the latent refinement process with rewards from longer-horizon imagined futures induced by latent plan edits. Empirical evaluations on the LIBERO benchmark demonstrate that PearlVLA achieves state-of-the-art performance among existing methods.

</details>


### [91] [Visual Verification Enables Inference-time Steering and Autonomous Policy Improvement](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18247v1)
*Mingtong Zhang,Dhruv Shah*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 机器人agent推理时验证与自我改进，可迁移至代码优化agent

TL;DR: 提出VERITAS框架，利用生成器-验证器在推理时评估动作，提升机器人策略性能，并通过验证的自生成轨迹实现高效的离线改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 机器人需要从经验中学习并持续改进，这要求一种实践和从反馈中学习的机制。

Method: 将预训练的通用机器人策略作为生成器，搭配无梯度的视觉验证器在推理时评估动作，实现推理时策略引导和自我改进。

Result: 推理时验证优于未用额外数据训练的通用策略；验证的rollout为离线策略改进提供有效监督，后训练性能与专家演示相当且无需人工干预。

Conclusion: 推理时验证是一种实用且可扩展的机制，可在部署过程中有效改进机器人策略。

中文摘要：部署在现实世界中的机器人应该从经验中学习并随着时间的推移不断改进。这需要一种实践和从反馈中学习的机制。在本文中，我们提出了VERITAS，一个用于通用机器人策略的生成器-验证器框架，用于推理时的策略引导和自我改进。我们使用一个预训练的通用机器人策略作为“生成器”，并将其与一个无梯度的“视觉验证器”配对，该验证器在推理时评估动作。该框架实现了推理时的引导，无需额外训练即可提高策略性能。我们证明了推理时验证始终优于在额外演示数据上未训练的普通通用策略。此外，我们证明了经过验证的 rollout 为离线策略改进提供了有效的监督：在验证的自我生成轨迹上微调的策略实现了持续的性能提升。值得注意的是，我们发现使用验证的 rollout 进行后训练达到了与专家演示相当的效果，同时不需要任何人工干预。我们的结果突出了推理时验证作为一种实用且可扩展的机制，用于在部署过程中改进机器人策略。

Original abstract: Robots deployed in the real world should learn from their experience and improve over time. This requires a mechanism of practicing and learning from feedback. In this paper, we propose VERITAS, a generator-verifier framework for generalist robot policies for inference-time policy steering and self-improvement. We use a pre-trained generalist robot policy as a ``generator'' and pair it with a gradient-free ``visual verifier'' that evaluates actions at inference time. This framework enables inference-time steering that improves policy performance without additional training. We demonstrate that inference-time verification consistently outperforms vanilla generalists without training on additional demonstration data. Additionally, we demonstrate that the verified rollouts provide effective supervision for offline policy improvement: policies fine-tuned on verified self-generated trajectories achieve consistent performance gains. Notably, we find that post-training with verified rollouts achieves comparable efficiency to expert demonstrations, while requiring no human interventions. Our results highlight inference-time verification as a practical and scalable mechanism for improving robotic policies during deployment.

</details>


### [92] [Guava: An Effective and Universal Harness for Embodied Manipulation](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18363v1)
*Haowen Liu,Xirui Li,Shaoxiong Yao,Peng Shi,Tianyi Zhou,Jia-Bin Huang,Furong Huang,Jiayuan Mao*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出通用agent harness框架，涉及工作流设计，可迁移至coding agent。

TL;DR: 提出Guava框架，通过迭代感知-推理-动作循环、语义动作抽象和多模态观测三个关键要素，利用不到2000条仿真轨迹将具身操作能力蒸馏到4B开源模型中，性能接近前沿专有模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前具身智能体通常采用端到端视觉-语言-动作系统或传统方法，但缺乏对有效驾驭框架的明确理解，以及这种框架对不同规模模型的普适性。

Method: 系统探索智能体工作流、动作空间和观测空间的设计空间，提出Guava框架，包含迭代感知-推理-动作循环、语义动作抽象和多模态观测；开发端到端训练流程，用少于2K仿真轨迹蒸馏到4B模型。

Result: 在仿真和真实环境中性能与前沿专有模型相当，对未见物体、新颖指令和长时域任务有强泛化。

Conclusion: 精心设计的驾驭框架可作为可扩展、模型无关的接口，使紧凑开源模型用极少训练数据实现强具身能力。

中文摘要：在大规模视觉-语言数据上训练的语言模型已展现出作为具身智能体的强大潜力。通过具身工具使用来驾驭模型，将高层推理与感知、规划和控制等外部模块相结合，为端到端的视觉-语言-动作系统提供了一种有前景的替代方案。然而，什么构成有效的具身操作驾驭框架，以及这种框架能在多大程度上解锁广泛推理模型的具身能力，仍不清楚。在本文中，我们提出了Guava，一个通过系统探索智能体工作流、动作空间和观测空间的设计空间而开发的具身工具使用驾驭框架。我们的研究确定了有效具身智能体的三个关键要素：迭代感知-推理-动作循环、语义动作抽象和多模态观测。为了理解这些设计原则是否对小型模型也具有普适性，我们开发了一个端到端训练流程，利用完全在仿真中收集的不到2000条轨迹，将具身操作能力蒸馏到一个4B开源模型中。在仿真和真实世界环境中的实验结果显示，其性能可与前沿专有模型相媲美，同时对未见过的物体、新颖指令和长时域任务展现出强大的泛化能力。结果表明，一个精心设计的驾驭框架可以作为具身操作的可扩展、模型无关的接口，在紧凑的开源模型中用极少的训练数据实现强大的新兴具身能力。

Original abstract: Language models trained on large-scale vision-language data have demonstrated strong potential for embodied agents. Harnessing models through embodied tools use offers a promising alternative to end-to-end vision-language-action systems by combining high-level reasoning with external modules for perception, planning, and control. However, it remains unclear what makes an effective harness for embodied manipulation, and to what extent such a harness can unlock embodied capabilities in a wide range of reasoning models. In this work, we present Guava, a harness framework for embodied tool use developed through systematic exploration of the design space of agent workflows, action spaces, and observation spaces. Our study identifies three key ingredients for effective embodied agents: iterative perception-reasoning-action loops, semantic action abstractions, and multimodal observations. To understand whether these design principles are universal even to small models, we develop an end-to-end training pipeline that distills embodied manipulation capabilities into a 4B open-source model using fewer than 2K trajectories collected entirely in simulation. Experimental results in both simulation and real-world environments show performance comparable to frontier proprietary models while exhibiting strong generalization to unseen objects, novel instructions, and long-horizon tasks. Results suggest that a well-designed harness can serve as a scalable, model-agnostic interface for embodied manipulation, enabling strong emergent embodied capabilities in compact open-source models with minimal training data.

</details>


### [93] [As You Wish: Mission Planning with Formal Verification using LLMs in Precision Agriculture](http://arxiv.org/abs/2606.18519v1)
*Marcos Abel Zuzuárregui,Stefano Carpin*

Main category: cs.RO

Selection reason: 提出基于LLM的任务规划系统，利用LTL进行形式化验证和反馈循环，可迁移至代码优化agent的验证与规划机制

TL;DR: 提出了一种利用LLM的精准农业任务规划系统，通过引入基于线性时序逻辑的反馈循环和双LLM架构来解决自然语言歧义问题，实验验证了方法有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器人系统操作复杂，需高级技能；之前的自然语言任务规划器存在歧义问题；需要确保规划满足用户规范。

Method: 在规划架构中引入多个基于线性时序逻辑的反馈循环，使用两个不同商业LLM分别负责规范生成和验证子任务以减轻偏见。

Result: 实验展示了该方法在生成有价值LTL公式方面的优势和局限，并验证了其解决歧义问题的能力。

Conclusion: 提出的集成任务验证的自主流水线有效提升了规划系统的规范符合性，但仍然存在LLM生成LTL公式的局限性。

中文摘要：尽管机器人系统现在正在各个行业中进行商业化和部署，但许多这些系统高度专业化，通常需要高级技能才能操作并确保它们按指令执行。为了缓解这个问题，我们最近引入了一个利用LLM的任务规划器，该规划器基于自然语言提供的任务描述来合成精准农业中的任务计划。虽然该系统表现出令人印象深刻的性能，但它也受到自然语言固有的歧义的影响。在本文中，我们扩展了我们的系统以解决这个问题，方法是在规划架构中引入多个反馈循环，利用线性时序逻辑（LTL）来确保任务规划系统满足用户制定的规范，同时仍然使用自然语言。为了减轻潜在偏见，这是通过使用两种不同的商业LLM来负责规范和验证子任务来实现的。通过大量实验，我们强调了将任务验证集成到完全自主流水线中的优势和局限，特别是关于LLM生成有价值的LTL公式的能力，并展示了我们提出的实现如何解决和克服这些挑战。

Original abstract: Though robotic systems are now being commercialized and deployed in various industries, many of these systems are highly specialized and often require an advanced skill set to operate and ensure they perform as instructed. To mitigate this problem, we recently introduced a mission planner leveraging LLMs to synthesize mission plans in precision agriculture based on mission descriptions provided in natural language. While the system demonstrates impressive performance, it also suffers from the inherent ambiguities of natural language. In this paper, we extend our system to address this issue by introducing multiple feedback loops in the planning architecture that leverage linear temporal logic (LTL) to ensure the mission planning system meets the specifications formulated by the user while still using natural language. To mitigate potential bias, this is achieved by using two different commercial LLMs in charge of the specification and verification subtasks. Through extensive experiments, we highlight the strengths and limitations of integrating mission verification into a fully autonomous pipeline, particularly regarding an LLM's ability to generate valuable LTL formulas, and show how our proposed implementation addresses and solves these challenges.

</details>
